if true; then \
  echo '#!/usr/bin/ocamlrun' > camlheader && \
  echo '#!/usr/bin/ocamlrun' > target_camlheader && \
  echo '#!/usr/bin/ocamlrund' > camlheaderd && \
  echo '#!/usr/bin/ocamlrund' > target_camlheaderd && \
  echo '#!' | tr -d '\012' > camlheader_ur; \
else \
  for suff in '' d; do \
    gcc -O -fno-defer-pop -Wall -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64 -D_REENTRANT -Wl,-E \
              -DRUNTIME_NAME='"/usr/bin/ocamlrun'$suff'"' \
              header.c -o tmpheader && \
    strip tmpheader && \
    mv tmpheader camlheader$suff && \
    gcc -O -fno-defer-pop -Wall -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64 -D_REENTRANT -Wl,-E \
              -DRUNTIME_NAME='"/usr/bin/ocamlrun'$suff'"' \
              header.c -o tmpheader && \
    strip tmpheader && \
    mv tmpheader target_camlheader$suff; \
  done && \
  cp camlheader camlheader_ur; \
fi
